 One such shrine of Shiva is Baijnath Dham
 kangra ke baijnath dham main mahadev ke sabase bade bhakt ne apni bhakthi kii pariksha di thi

 himachal kii khubasurat or hari-bhari vaadiyon main dhauladhar parvat shrinkhalaaon ke bich basaa pracheen shiv mandir mahadev ke sabase bade bhakt kii bhakthi kii kahani sunata he
 This Shivling is established here, which is like any common Shivling
 lekin iskaa sparsh bhakton ko anoothaa ehsaas detaa he

 kivdantiyon kii maane to ravan isi shivlinga ko apane saath lanka le janaa chahta tha
 Baijnath Dham is situated on the banks of the Binwa River, 54 km from Kangra in Himachal and 56 km from Dharamshala
 jo apane chaaron ore maujuud prakritik sundarataa kii vajah se ek vishisht sthaan rakhata he
 It is said that in the 12th century, two merchants named Manyuk and Ahuk built this temple, after which the temple was renovated in Raja Sansar Chand
 puranic manyata ke anusaar treta yug main ravan ne shivaji kii tapasya kii thi

 dasvaan or antim sir cat jane se pehle shivaji ne prakat hokar ravan kaa haath pakad liya or ek vaidya kii tarah hi ravan ke sabhi siron ko pun:sthapit kar diya

 usne baiju naam ke gwaale ko sab baat samajhakar shivlinga pakada die or shankaa nivaaran ke liye chalaa gaya

 is tarah donon shivlinga vahiin sthapit ho gaye

 inkaa ashtami ke din pujan kaa vidhaan he
 He is worshiped by the whole world
 maa mahagauri param kalyankari hai
 She is the idol of Mamta and will fulfill all the needs of the devotees
 pujan karne se samast paapon kaa kshay hokar kanti badhati he, sukh main vruddhi hoti he, lekin sabase badi baat ye he ki agar aap aarthik ksht se pareshaan hai, to maa mahagauri kii puja aapke aarthik kami kii pareshaani ko dur kar sakati he
 Apart from this, Mahagauri can also get the boon of desired marriage
 devi mahagauri ke swaroop kii mahima kya he-navaratri ke aathven din devi mahagauri kii puja archana kii jaati he
 She is named Mahagauri due to the color of the Goddess
 mahagauri kii puja archana se purv janm ke paap nasht hone ke saath-saath is janm ke dukh daridrata or ksht bhi mit jate he
 Goddess Mahagauri has four arms and Taurus is her vehicle
 daaen haath main abhaya mudra or neeche vaale daaen haath me trishul he
 There is damru in the top left hand and var mudra in the bottom left hand
 devi mahagauri kii puja archana se kundali kaa kamjor shukr majboot hota he
 Therefore, Mahagauri is worshiped to remove the problems faced in marriage
 mahagauri kii puja archana se daanpaty jivan sukhad hota he saath hi paariwarik kalah klesh khatm hoti hai
 What is the significance of the eighth day of Navratri? - On the eighth day of Navratri, one can get the boon of early marriage
 - saath hi vaivaahik jivan bhi sukhmay ho saktaa he
 - On this day, Mother Mahagauri is worshiped as the eighth form of Mother
 - mana jaataa he ki mata sita ne shri ram kii prapti ke liye inhen kii puja kii thi
 - In order to remove all the obstacles related to marriage, their worship is perfect
 - jyotish main inkaa sambandh shukr naamak grah se mana jaataa he
 What is the worship method of Maa Gauri? - Start worship by wearing yellow clothes
 - maa ke samaksh deepak jalaaen or unka dhyaan karen
 - Offer white or yellow flowers to the mother in worship
 - uske baad inke mantron kaa jaap karen
 If the worship is done in the middle of the night, the results will be more auspicious
 vivaah kii baadha dur karne ke liye aise karen devi mahagauri kii puja archana-- lakdi ke patare par svachh pilaa vastra bichhaakar devi mahagauri kii pratimaa ko sthapit karen
 - By wearing yellow clothes yourself, sanctify the entire place of worship with Ganga water
 - devi mahagauri ke saamne gaay ke ghi kaa diya jalaaen or unka dhyaan karen
 - Offer white or yellow flowers to the Goddess with both hands and chant the mantra
 - yaa devi sarvbhooteshu maa mahagauri roopen sansthitanmastasye namastasye namastasye namo namah- nimna mantra kaa 27 yaa 54 baar jaap karne se vivaah main aa rahi sari baadhaaen dur hoti hai- prasad ke rup main devi mahagauri ko nariyal arpan karen
 - By doing this, you will get the desired fruit and girls get a suitable groom
 raatri kaa mahoupaay dengi mahagauri mahaavardaan-- ek safed asana par baithkar mahagauri ke saamne gaay ke ghi kaa diya jalaaen or tambe ke lote main jal bharkar rakhen
 - Read Shri Durga Saptashati and offer white sweetmeats and coconut
 - paath puraa hone ke baad jal ko saare ghar main chhidak den or prasad ke rup main nariyal khaaen
 - Doing this will end family strife
 har kaary main safalataa milegi

 - maa ko safed phool, or safed mithai arpit karen
 - Then chant "om Shun Shukraay Namah", the basic mantra of Venus
 - shukr kii samasyaon ke samaapti kii prarthana karen

 com Bhasha Singh's book Invisible India is not just an encounter with the stark reality of manual scavenging, as shown on its front page by its title and sub-title, but also by the harsh experiences of the caste system rooted in Indian society and its mindset
 There is an escorted encounter of passing
 is sabko bhashaa ne gahan samvednaa or saamaajik yatharth ke saath pesh kiya he
 The encounter is also in the sense that when language meets families associated with the profession of scavenging, then a question with its full nudity is from Patna to Gujarat, West Bengal, Ambala, Kanpur, Kashmir, ie wherever the writer went
 There this question was asked in some form or the other, sometimes straight and sometimes twisting around - "who is going?" You don't feel like our caste
 ‚Äùbhashaa ke liye yah sawaal gambhir muddon or sarokaaron se judye jaisaa tha
 In this journey of the writer's own journalism, such experiences lead him to many conclusions and become a harsh truth of Indian life
 bhashaa ne mailaa dhone kii pratha kaa surveykshan, adhyayan, jise ve adrishy bharat kah rahi hai, 2003 se 2011 ke bich kiya tha
 In this study, when she tries to look at this problem with personal experiences, there are some aspects of truth which are known to be consciously ignored
 lekhika kahati hai, ''yah duniya itani adrishy he ki maine khud 33 saal kii umr ke baad hi ise jatigat kupratha ke rup main mahasoos kiya, jabaki aisa nahin ki yah pehle kabhi mere agal-bagal nahin rahi
 From my upbringing city Lucknow to Kanpur, Allahabad, Patna, scavenging women have been everywhere and remained unaware of their presence
 sabase pehle maine ise elahabaad main dekha
 "(bhumika, p
 21) The way in which the language scripts the bitter truth of this practice presents a squalid picture of Indian life:" Whether it is the Lakshmaniya Hari of Bhatpada in North 24 Parganas district of West Bengal or in Gujarat
 Pallavi Ben of Ahmedabad, Indira of Tonk in Rajasthan, Rafika of Kashmir or Narayanamma of Andhra Pradesh all came to the same conclusion after spending their lives in manual scavenging Hunchin that people do not consider them human beings and the government do not appear because she does not want to see them
 
 
 ‚Äùapane swayan ke tamaam anubhavon ko bhashaa ne is kitaab main puri sachaai or eemaandaaree se darj kiya he
 That is why, when this book comes out as a document of this hellish torture, the mind is really pained by deep pain and painful truth
 jis sachaai ko sirf mailaa dhone vaala hi jaanata tha, use bhoga rahaa tha, baaki samaaj use nirpeksh bhav se dekhakar aage bad jaataa tha kyonki yah uski soch or maansikta main hi nahin tha ki safaikarmi bhi ek insaan he
 In the second part of the book, the truth of the Government of India's program, rehabilitation, law, etc
 has also been presented seriously through this book
 yah behad prabhaavshaalee bana he
 The society not only creates deep admiration for manual scavenging but also questions the thinking, mindset and system of the society with seriousness
 is pratha ke prati man main ek gussa paidaa hota he, jo pathakon ko bheetar tak hilaa detaa he
 This book brings out the serious study of Bhasha Singh and his generosity towards humanity
 yah bhartiya jivan ko ek aisa aainaa dikhaati he, jahaan bharat kii kalushita, vidrupata or amanviyata kii nagn tasviir ubhartee he
 Like a vile stain that appears to encounter the Indian social system directly
